;; DeductionMatch and ImplicationDirectionIntroductionMatch
!(import! &self ImplicationDirectIntroductionMatch.metta)

%~ load_answer_file( '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/compat/match/DeductionImplicationDirectIntroductionMatchTest.metta.answers',

;;; MeTTa port of the Implication Direct Introduction PLN rule, using
;;; the match operator.
;;;
;;; (P a)  p
;;; ...
;;; (P a)  p
;;; (Q a)  q
;;; ...
;;; (Q a)  q
;;; 
;;; PQ  tv
;;;
;;; where p (resp. q) are of boolean type representing whether (P a)
;;; (resp. (Q a)) has been observed as True or False, and tv
;;; represents the resulting truth value of the conclusion.
;; Import modules
!(import! &self "../common/OrderedSet.metta")

%~ ../common/OrderedSet.metta:1 
%~ load_answer_file( '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/compat/match/DeductionImplicationDirectIntroductionMatchTest.metta.answers',
%~   '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/compat/match/DeductionImplicationDirectIntroductionMatchTest.metta')
;;; Import modules
!(import! &self Num.metta)

%~ load_answer_file( '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/compat/match/DeductionImplicationDirectIntroductionMatchTest.metta.answers',
%~   '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/compat/match/DeductionImplicationDirectIntroductionMatchTest.metta')
;; Definition of a set data structure.  Under the hood it is a sorted
;; list without duplicates, thus called OrderedSet.  For now its
;; constructor :: is unconstrained, meaning it does not guaranty that
;; the constructed OrderedSet are sorted and without duplicates.
;; Rather this is delegated to the insert function defined below.  In
;; order to guaranty that it is sorted without duplicates, the
;; constructor :: would need to take an additional argument encoding a
;; proof that the element to prepend is less than the head of the set
;; to be prepended to.
;;; Collection of functions operating on numbers
;; Define max
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,max,[->,A,A,A]])
  (: max 
    (-> $A $A $A))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[max,X,Y],[if,[>,X,Y],X,Y])
  (= 
    (max $X $Y) 
    (if 
      (> $X $Y) $X $Y))


;; Define min
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,min,[->,A,A,A]])
  (: min 
    (-> $A $A $A))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[min,X,Y],[if,[<,X,Y],X,Y])
  (= 
    (min $X $Y) 
    (if 
      (< $X $Y) $X $Y))


;; Clamp a number to be within a certain range
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,clamp,[->,A,A,A,A]])
  (: clamp 
    (-> $A $A $A $A))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[clamp,X,L,U],[max,L,[min,U,X]])
  (= 
    (clamp $X $L $U) 
    (max $L 
      (min $U $X)))


;; Define abs
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,abs,[->,A,A]])
  (: abs 
    (-> $A $A))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[abs,X],[if,[<,X,0],[*,-1,X],X])
  (= 
    (abs $X) 
    (if 
      (< $X 0) 
      (* -1 $X) $X))


;; Define <=
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,<=,[->,A,A,'Bool']])
  (: <= 
    (-> $A $A Bool))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[<=,X,Y],[or,[<,X,Y],[==,X,Y]])
  (= 
    (<= $X $Y) 
    (or 
      (< $X $Y) 
      (== $X $Y)))


;; Define >=
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,>=,[->,A,A,'Bool']])
  (: >= 
    (-> $A $A Bool))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[>=,X,Y],[or,[>,X,Y],[==,X,Y]])
  (= 
    (>= $X $Y) 
    (or 
      (> $X $Y) 
      (== $X $Y)))


;; Define approximately equal
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,approxEq,[->,A,A,A,'Bool']])
  (: approxEq 
    (-> $A $A $A Bool))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[approxEq,X,Y,Epsilon],[<=,[abs,[-,X,Y]],Epsilon])
  (= 
    (approxEq $X $Y $Epsilon) 
    (<= 
      (abs 
        (- $X $Y)) $Epsilon))


;; Define Nat
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'Nat','Type'])
  (: Nat Type)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'Z','Nat'])
  (: Z Nat)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'S',[->,'Nat','Nat']])
  (: S 
    (-> Nat Nat))


;; Define cast functions between Nat and Number
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,fromNumber,[->,'Number','Nat']])
  (: fromNumber 
    (-> Number Nat))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[fromNumber,N],[if,[<=,N,0],'Z',['S',[fromNumber,[-,N,1]]]])
  (= 
    (fromNumber $N) 
    (if 
      (<= $N 0) Z 
      (S 
        (fromNumber 
          (- $N 1)))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,fromNat,[->,'Nat','Number']])
  (: fromNat 
    (-> Nat Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[fromNat,'Z'],0)
  (= 
    (fromNat Z) 0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[fromNat,['S',K]],[+,1,[fromNat,K]])
  (= 
    (fromNat 
      (S $K)) 
    (+ 1 
      (fromNat $K)))


;; Define a generic less than operator, , for Nat.  < cannot be used
;; because it is a built-in, its type is hardwired and cannot be
;; overloaded.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'',[->,'Nat','Nat','Bool']])
  (:  
    (-> Nat Nat Bool))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['',_,'Z'],'False')
  (= 
    ( $_ Z) False)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['','Z',['S',_]],'True')
  (= 
    ( Z 
      (S $_)) True)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['',['S',X],['S',Y]],['',X,Y])
  (= 
    ( 
      (S $X) 
      (S $Y)) 
    ( $X $Y))


;; Overload  for Number.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'',[->,'Number','Number','Bool']])
  (:  
    (-> Number Number Bool))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['',X,Y],[<,X,Y])
  (= 
    ( $X $Y) 
    (< $X $Y))


;; Return the ceiling of a non negative number.  If the number is
;; negative it returns 1.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,ceil,[->,'Number','Number']])
  (: ceil 
    (-> Number Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[ceil,N],[fromNat,[fromNumber,N]])
  (= 
    (ceil $N) 
    (fromNat 
      (fromNumber $N)))


;; Convert Number to Bool.  Anything above 0 converts to True.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'number->bool',[->,'Number','Bool']])
  (: number->bool 
    (-> Number Bool))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['number->bool',X],[<,0,X])
  (= 
    (number->bool $X) 
    (< 0 $X))


;; Convert Bool to Number.  False converts to 0, True converts to 1.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'bool->number',[->,'Bool','Number']])
  (: bool->number 
    (-> Bool Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['bool->number','False'],0)
  (= 
    (bool->number False) 0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['bool->number','True'],1)
  (= 
    (bool->number True) 1)


;; Define a less than type.  Note that it is purposefully different
;; than  as it is a type, not an operator.  Inhabitants of ( x y)
;; are proofs that x  y == True.  For now  is only axiomatized for
;; Nat.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'\x8D\\x83\',[->,True,True,'Type']])
  (:  
    (-> $True $True Type))


;; Zero is always less than the successor of something
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,['zero-lt-succ-axiom'],[->,'Atom']])
  (: 
    (zero-lt-succ-axiom) 
    (-> Atom))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['zero-lt-succ-axiom'],[:,'ZeroLTSucc',['\x8D\\x83\','Z',['S',K]]])
  (= 
    (zero-lt-succ-axiom) 
    (: ZeroLTSucc 
      ( Z 
        (S $K))))


;; If x  y then (S x)  (S y)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,['succ-monotonicity-rule'],[->,'Atom']])
  (: 
    (succ-monotonicity-rule) 
    (-> Atom))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['succ-monotonicity-rule'],[:,'SuccMonotonicity',[->,['\x8D\\x83\',X,Y],['\x8D\\x83\',['S',X],['S',Y]]]])
  (= 
    (succ-monotonicity-rule) 
    (: SuccMonotonicity 
      (-> 
        ( $X $Y) 
        ( 
          (S $X) 
          (S $Y)))))


; Evaluation took 275.31 ms.

  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'OrderedSet',[->,A,'Type']])
  (: OrderedSet 
    (-> $A Type))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'\x88\\x85\',['OrderedSet',A]])
  (:  
    (OrderedSet $A))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,::,[->,A,['OrderedSet',A],['OrderedSet',A]]])
  (: :: 
    (-> $A 
      (OrderedSet $A) 
      (OrderedSet $A)))


;; Check if an element is in a set.  TODO: optimize assuming it is
;; ordered.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,elem,[->,A,['OrderedSet',A],'Bool']])
  (: elem 
    (-> $A 
      (OrderedSet $A) Bool))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[elem,X,'\x88\\x85\'],'False')
  (= 
    (elem $X ) False)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[elem,X,[::,H,True]],[if,[==,X,H],'True',[elem,X,True]])
  (= 
    (elem $X 
      (:: $H $True)) 
    (if 
      (== $X $H) True 
      (elem $X $True)))


;; Insert an element into a set.  Only insert if the element is not
;; already in the set as to produce an ordered set.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,insert,[->,A,['OrderedSet',A],['OrderedSet',A]]])
  (: insert 
    (-> $A 
      (OrderedSet $A) 
      (OrderedSet $A)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[insert,X,'\x88\\x85\'],[::,X,'\x88\\x85\'])
  (= 
    (insert $X ) 
    (:: $X ))


; Base case
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[insert,X,[::,H,True]],[if,[==,X,H],[::,H,True],[if,['',X,H],[::,X,[::,H,True]],[::,H,[insert,X,True]]]])
  (= 
    (insert $X 
      (:: $H $True)) 
    (if 
      (== $X $H) 
      (:: $H $True) 
      (if 
        ( $X $H) 
        (:: $X 
          (:: $H $True)) 
        (:: $H 
          (insert $X $True)))))

  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'Pr',[->,'Number','TruthValue']])

;; Second order probability TV constructor, i.e. probability and
;; count.  The second order probability is distributed according to a
;; beta distribution.  The first argument of the constructor
;; represents the mode of the second order distribution.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'PrCnt',[->,'Number','Number','TruthValue']])

    (-> Number Number TruthValue))


;; Simple Truth Value.  A Second order probability TV constructor,
;; i.e. probability and confidence.  The probability is in fact the
;; mode of the corresponding beta distribution.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'STV',[->,'Number','Number','TruthValue']])
  (: STV 
    (-> Number Number TruthValue))

;; Constants ;;

  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[prior_alpha],0.5)

  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[lookahead],1.0)
  (= 
    (lookahead) 1.0)


;; Maximum supported count (till +inf is supported, possibly).
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'max-count',[->,'Number']])
  (: max-count 
    (-> Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['max-count'],1000000000.0)
  (= 
    (max-count) 1000000000.0)


;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; Methods ;;
;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; Convert count to confidence using the formula
;;
;; confidence = count / (count + lookahead)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'count->confidence',[->,'Number','Number']])
  (: count->confidence 
    (-> Number Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['count->confidence',Cnt],[/,Cnt,[+,Cnt,[lookahead]]])
  (= 
    (count->confidence $Cnt) 
    (/ $Cnt 
      (+ $Cnt 
        (lookahead))))


;; Convert confidence to count using the formula
;;
;; count = (confidence * lookahead) / (1 - confidence)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'confidence->count',[->,'Number','Number']])
  (: confidence->count 
    (-> Number Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['confidence->count',Conf],[if,[approxEq,1.0,Conf,1.0e-9],['max-count'],[/,[*,Conf,[lookahead]],[-,1.0,Conf]]])
  (= 
    (confidence->count $Conf) 
    (if 
      (approxEq 1.0 $Conf 1.0e-9) 
      (max-count) 
      (/ 
        (* $Conf 
          (lookahead)) 
        (- 1.0 $Conf))))


;; Increment the given count by 1
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'inc-count',[->,'Number','Number']])
  (: inc-count 
    (-> Number Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['inc-count',Cnt],[+,1,Cnt])
  (= 
    (inc-count $Cnt) 
    (+ 1 $Cnt))


;; Increment the corresponding count of the given confidence by 1 and
;; return the confidence of that corresponding incremented count.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'inc-confidence',[->,'Number','Number']])
  (: inc-confidence 
    (-> Number Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['inc-confidence',Conf],['count->confidence',['inc-count',['confidence->count',Conf]]])
  (= 
    (inc-confidence $Conf) 
    (count->confidence 
      (inc-count 
        (confidence->count $Conf))))


;; Return the strength of a truth value, given that its count has been
;; incremented by one but its positive count has not.
;;
;; The formula is derived from new_s = s*cnt / (cnt + 1), where cnt is
;; the count of the original truth value, that is cnt = c*k / (1-c).
;; Thus
;;
;; new_s = (s*c*k / (1-c)) / (c*k / (1-c) + 1)
;;       = (s*c*k / (1-c)) / ((c*k + 1-c) / (1-c))
;;       = (s*c*k) / (c*k + 1-c)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'inc-count-strength',[->,'Number','Number','Number']])
  (: inc-count-strength 
    (-> Number Number Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['inc-count-strength',S,C],[/,[*,S,[*,C,[lookahead]]],[-,[+,[*,C,[lookahead]],1],C]])
  (= 
    (inc-count-strength $S $C) 
    (/ 
      (* $S 
        (* $C 
          (lookahead))) 
      (- 
        (+ 
          (* $C 
            (lookahead)) 1) $C)))


;; Return the first order probability mode of the second order
;; distribution associated to a truth value.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,mode,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: mode 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mode,['Bl','True']],1.0)
  (= 
    (mode 
      (Bl True)) 1.0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mode,['Bl','False']],0.0)
  (= 
    (mode 
      (Bl False)) 0.0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mode,['Pr',Pr]],Pr)
  (= 
    (mode 
      (Pr $Pr)) $Pr)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mode,['PrCnt',Pr,_]],Pr)
  (= 
    (mode 
      (PrCnt $Pr $_)) $Pr)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mode,['STV',Pr,_]],Pr)
  (= 
    (mode 
      (STV $Pr $_)) $Pr)


;; Return the total count of a truth value.  For truth values not
;; capturing a notion of confidence, such as Bl or Pr then the count
;; is assumed to be a very large number (cause +inf does not seem to
;; be supported at the moment).  For truth values capturing a notion
;; of confidence, such as PrCnt, the total count is the count
;; component of the truth value.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,count,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: count 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[count,['Bl',_]],['max-count'])
  (= 
    (count 
      (Bl $_)) 
    (max-count))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[count,['Pr',_]],['max-count'])
  (= 
    (count 
      (Pr $_)) 
    (max-count))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[count,['PrCnt',_,Cnt]],Cnt)
  (= 
    (count 
      (PrCnt $_ $Cnt)) $Cnt)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[count,['STV',_,Conf]],['confidence->count',Conf])
  (= 
    (count 
      (STV $_ $Conf)) 
    (confidence->count $Conf))


;; Return the confidence of a truth value.  For truth values not
;; capturing a notion of confidence, such as Bl or Pr then the
;; confidence is assumed to be 1.0.  For truth values capturing a
;; notion of confidence, such as PrCnt, the formula to convert a count
;; into confidence is as follows
;;
;; confidence = count / (count + lookahead)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,confidence,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: confidence 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[confidence,['Bl',_]],1.0)
  (= 
    (confidence 
      (Bl $_)) 1.0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[confidence,['Pr',_]],1.0)
  (= 
    (confidence 
      (Pr $_)) 1.0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[confidence,['PrCnt',_,Cnt]],['count->confidence',Cnt])
  (= 
    (confidence 
      (PrCnt $_ $Cnt)) 
    (count->confidence $Cnt))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[confidence,['STV',_,Conf]],Conf)
  (= 
    (confidence 
      (STV $_ $Conf)) $Conf)


;; Return the positive count of a truth value.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,pos_count,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: pos_count 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[pos_count,Tv],[*,[mode,Tv],[count,Tv]])
  (= 
    (pos_count $Tv) 
    (* 
      (mode $Tv) 
      (count $Tv)))


;; Return the negative count of a truth value.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,neg_count,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: neg_count 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[neg_count,Tv],[*,[-,1,[mode,Tv]],[count,Tv]])
  (= 
    (neg_count $Tv) 
    (* 
      (- 1 
        (mode $Tv)) 
      (count $Tv)))


;; Return the posterior alpha of a truth value
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,post_alpha,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: post_alpha 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[post_alpha,Tv],[+,[prior_alpha],[pos_count,Tv]])
  (= 
    (post_alpha $Tv) 
    (+ 
      (prior_alpha) 
      (pos_count $Tv)))


;; Return the posterior beta of a truth value
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,post_beta,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: post_beta 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[post_beta,Tv],[+,[prior_beta],[neg_count,Tv]])
  (= 
    (post_beta $Tv) 
    (+ 
      (prior_beta) 
      (neg_count $Tv)))


;; Return the first order probability mean of the second order
;; distribution associated to a truth value.  For truth values not
;; capturing a notion of confidence, such as Bl or Pr then the
;; confidence is assumed to be 1.0.  For truth values capturing a
;; notion of confidence, such as PrCnt, a beta distribution is
;; assumed.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,mean,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: mean 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mean,['Bl','True']],1.0)
  (= 
    (mean 
      (Bl True)) 1.0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mean,['Bl','False']],0.0)
  (= 
    (mean 
      (Bl False)) 0.0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mean,['Pr',Pr]],Pr)
  (= 
    (mean 
      (Pr $Pr)) $Pr)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mean,['PrCnt',Pr,Cnt]],['let*',[[A,[post_alpha,['PrCnt',Pr,Cnt]]],[B,[post_beta,['PrCnt',Pr,Cnt]]]],[/,A,[+,A,B]]])
  (=

  (= 
    (mean 
      (STV $Pr $Conf)) 
    (let*

        (+ $A $B))))

;; Definition of a set data structure.  Under the hood it is a sorted
;; list without duplicates, thus called OrderedSet.  For now its
;; constructor :: is unconstrained, meaning it does not guaranty that
;; the constructed OrderedSet are sorted and without duplicates.
;; Rather this is delegated to the insert function defined below.  In
;; order to guaranty that it is sorted without duplicates, the
;; constructor :: would need to take an additional argument encoding a
;; proof that the element to prepend is less than the head of the set
;; to be prepended to.
;;; Collection of functions operating on numbers
;; Define max
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,max,[->,A,A,A]])
  (: max 
    (-> $A $A $A))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[max,X,Y],[if,[>,X,Y],X,Y])
  (= 
    (max $X $Y) 
    (if 
      (> $X $Y) $X $Y))


;; Define min
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,min,[->,A,A,A]])
  (: min 
    (-> $A $A $A))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[min,X,Y],[if,[<,X,Y],X,Y])
  (= 
    (min $X $Y) 
    (if 
      (< $X $Y) $X $Y))


;; Clamp a number to be within a certain range
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,clamp,[->,A,A,A,A]])
  (: clamp 
    (-> $A $A $A $A))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[clamp,X,L,U],[max,L,[min,U,X]])
  (= 
    (clamp $X $L $U) 
    (max $L 
      (min $U $X)))


;; Define abs
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,abs,[->,A,A]])
  (: abs 
    (-> $A $A))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[abs,X],[if,[<,X,0],[*,-1,X],X])
  (= 
    (abs $X) 
    (if 
      (< $X 0) 
      (* -1 $X) $X))


;; Define <=
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,<=,[->,A,A,'Bool']])
  (: <= 
    (-> $A $A Bool))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[<=,X,Y],[or,[<,X,Y],[==,X,Y]])
  (= 
    (<= $X $Y) 
    (or 
      (< $X $Y) 
      (== $X $Y)))


;; Define >=
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,>=,[->,A,A,'Bool']])
  (: >= 
    (-> $A $A Bool))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[>=,X,Y],[or,[>,X,Y],[==,X,Y]])
  (= 
    (>= $X $Y) 
    (or 
      (> $X $Y) 
      (== $X $Y)))


;; Define approximately equal
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,approxEq,[->,A,A,A,'Bool']])
  (: approxEq 
    (-> $A $A $A Bool))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[approxEq,X,Y,Epsilon],[<=,[abs,[-,X,Y]],Epsilon])
  (= 
    (approxEq $X $Y $Epsilon) 
    (<= 
      (abs 
        (- $X $Y)) $Epsilon))

  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,fromNumber,[->,'Number','Nat']])

  (=

    (if 
      (<= $N 0) Z

        (fromNumber

  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,fromNat,[->,'Nat','Number']])

;; Define a generic less than operator, , for Nat.  < cannot be used

  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'',[->,'Nat','Nat','Bool']])

  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,['succ-monotonicity-rule'],[->,'Atom']])
  (:

  (: post_beta

  (= 
    (post_beta 
      (ETV $Ev $Tv))

      (prior_beta) 
      (neg_count $Tv)))

;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; Rule Definition ;;
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; To deal with an abritrary number of pieces of evidence the rule is
;; defined inductively.
;; Base case (axiomatic rule):
;;
;; pq  (ETV Empty (PrCnt 1 0))
;;
;; Directly present in the atomspace.
;;; Formula for the inductive Implication Direct Introduction rule.
;; Import modules
!(import! &self "../truthvalue/TruthValue.metta")

  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,max,[->,A,A,A]])

  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[max,X,Y],[if,[>,X,Y],X,Y])
  (= 
    (max $X $Y) 
    (if 
      (> $X $Y) $X $Y))

  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,min,[->,A,A,A]])

      (< $X $Y) $X $Y))

    (clamp $X $L $U) 
    (max $L 
      (min $U $X)))

  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[approxEq,X,Y,Epsilon],[<=,[abs,[-,X,Y]],Epsilon])
  (=

  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'',[->,'Nat','Nat','Bool']])

  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'\x8D\\x83\',[->,True,True,'Type']])

;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; Constructors ;;
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; Boolean TV constructor
;; TODO: alternatively we could have (:  TruthValue) and (:  TruthValue)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'Bl',[->,'Bool','TruthValue']])
  (: Bl 
    (-> Bool TruthValue))


;; First order probability TV constructor, i.e. mere probability.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'Pr',[->,'Number','TruthValue']])
  (: Pr 
    (-> Number TruthValue))


;; Second order probability TV constructor, i.e. probability and
;; count.  The second order probability is distributed according to a
;; beta distribution.  The first argument of the constructor
;; represents the mode of the second order distribution.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'PrCnt',[->,'Number','Number','TruthValue']])
  (: PrCnt 
    (-> Number Number TruthValue))


;; Simple Truth Value.  A Second order probability TV constructor,
;; i.e. probability and confidence.  The probability is in fact the
;; mode of the corresponding beta distribution.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'STV',[->,'Number','Number','TruthValue']])
  (: STV 
    (-> Number Number TruthValue))


;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; Constants ;;
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; For now the underlying beta distributions have a Jeffreys prior,
;; i.e. the prior alpha and beta are 0.5.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,prior_alpha,[->,'Number']])
  (: prior_alpha 
    (-> Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[prior_alpha],0.5)
  (= 
    (prior_alpha) 0.5)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,prior_beta,[->,'Number']])
  (: prior_beta 
    (-> Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[prior_beta],0.5)
  (= 
    (prior_beta) 0.5)


;; Lookahead
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,lookahead,[->,'Number']])
  (: lookahead 
    (-> Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[lookahead],1.0)
  (= 
    (lookahead) 1.0)


;; Maximum supported count (till +inf is supported, possibly).
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'max-count',[->,'Number']])
  (: max-count 
    (-> Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['max-count'],1000000000.0)
  (= 
    (max-count) 1000000000.0)


;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; Methods ;;
;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; Convert count to confidence using the formula
;;
;; confidence = count / (count + lookahead)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'count->confidence',[->,'Number','Number']])
  (: count->confidence 
    (-> Number Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['count->confidence',Cnt],[/,Cnt,[+,Cnt,[lookahead]]])
  (= 
    (count->confidence $Cnt) 
    (/ $Cnt 
      (+ $Cnt 
        (lookahead))))


;; Convert confidence to count using the formula
;;
;; count = (confidence * lookahead) / (1 - confidence)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'confidence->count',[->,'Number','Number']])
  (: confidence->count 
    (-> Number Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['confidence->count',Conf],[if,[approxEq,1.0,Conf,1.0e-9],['max-count'],[/,[*,Conf,[lookahead]],[-,1.0,Conf]]])
  (= 
    (confidence->count $Conf) 
    (if 
      (approxEq 1.0 $Conf 1.0e-9) 
      (max-count) 
      (/ 
        (* $Conf 
          (lookahead)) 
        (- 1.0 $Conf))))


;; Increment the given count by 1
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'inc-count',[->,'Number','Number']])
  (: inc-count 
    (-> Number Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['inc-count',Cnt],[+,1,Cnt])
  (= 
    (inc-count $Cnt) 
    (+ 1 $Cnt))


;; Increment the corresponding count of the given confidence by 1 and
;; return the confidence of that corresponding incremented count.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'inc-confidence',[->,'Number','Number']])
  (: inc-confidence 
    (-> Number Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['inc-confidence',Conf],['count->confidence',['inc-count',['confidence->count',Conf]]])
  (= 
    (inc-confidence $Conf) 
    (count->confidence 
      (inc-count 
        (confidence->count $Conf))))


;; Return the strength of a truth value, given that its count has been
;; incremented by one but its positive count has not.
;;
;; The formula is derived from new_s = s*cnt / (cnt + 1), where cnt is
;; the count of the original truth value, that is cnt = c*k / (1-c).
;; Thus
;;
;; new_s = (s*c*k / (1-c)) / (c*k / (1-c) + 1)
;;       = (s*c*k / (1-c)) / ((c*k + 1-c) / (1-c))
;;       = (s*c*k) / (c*k + 1-c)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'inc-count-strength',[->,'Number','Number','Number']])
  (: inc-count-strength 
    (-> Number Number Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['inc-count-strength',S,C],[/,[*,S,[*,C,[lookahead]]],[-,[+,[*,C,[lookahead]],1],C]])
  (= 
    (inc-count-strength $S $C) 
    (/ 
      (* $S 
        (* $C 
          (lookahead))) 
      (- 
        (+ 
          (* $C 
            (lookahead)) 1) $C)))


;; Return the first order probability mode of the second order
;; distribution associated to a truth value.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,mode,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: mode 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mode,['Bl','True']],1.0)
  (= 
    (mode 
      (Bl True)) 1.0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mode,['Bl','False']],0.0)
  (= 
    (mode 
      (Bl False)) 0.0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mode,['Pr',Pr]],Pr)
  (= 
    (mode 
      (Pr $Pr)) $Pr)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mode,['PrCnt',Pr,_]],Pr)
  (= 
    (mode 
      (PrCnt $Pr $_)) $Pr)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mode,['STV',Pr,_]],Pr)
  (= 
    (mode 
      (STV $Pr $_)) $Pr)


;; Return the total count of a truth value.  For truth values not
;; capturing a notion of confidence, such as Bl or Pr then the count
;; is assumed to be a very large number (cause +inf does not seem to
;; be supported at the moment).  For truth values capturing a notion
;; of confidence, such as PrCnt, the total count is the count
;; component of the truth value.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,count,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: count 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[count,['Bl',_]],['max-count'])
  (= 
    (count 
      (Bl $_)) 
    (max-count))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[count,['Pr',_]],['max-count'])
  (= 
    (count 
      (Pr $_)) 
    (max-count))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[count,['PrCnt',_,Cnt]],Cnt)
  (= 
    (count 
      (PrCnt $_ $Cnt)) $Cnt)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[count,['STV',_,Conf]],['confidence->count',Conf])
  (= 
    (count 
      (STV $_ $Conf)) 
    (confidence->count $Conf))


;; Return the confidence of a truth value.  For truth values not
;; capturing a notion of confidence, such as Bl or Pr then the
;; confidence is assumed to be 1.0.  For truth values capturing a
;; notion of confidence, such as PrCnt, the formula to convert a count

  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,confidence,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])

  (= 
    (confidence 
      (PrCnt $_ $Cnt)) 
    (count->confidence $Cnt))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[confidence,['STV',_,Conf]],Conf)
  (= 
    (confidence 
      (STV $_ $Conf)) $Conf)


;; Return the positive count of a truth value.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,pos_count,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: pos_count

  (=

    (* 
      (mode $Tv)

  (=

;; Return the first order probability mean of the second order
;; distribution associated to a truth value.  For truth values not
;; capturing a notion of confidence, such as Bl or Pr then the
;; confidence is assumed to be 1.0.  For truth values capturing a
;; notion of confidence, such as PrCnt, a beta distribution is

  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,mean,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: mean

  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mean,['Bl','True']],1.0)

  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mean,['Bl','False']],0.0)
  (=

  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mean,['Pr',Pr]],Pr)
  (=

      (Pr $Pr)) $Pr)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mean,['PrCnt',Pr,Cnt]],['let*',[[A,[post_alpha,['PrCnt',Pr,Cnt]]],[B,[post_beta,['PrCnt',Pr,Cnt]]]],[/,A,[+,A,B]]])

  (=

        (+ $A $B))))

;; Alternate implication direct introduction formula.  Inductive case,
;; meaning the piece of evidence gets aggregated to another truth
;; value.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'direct-introduction-recursive-formula',[->,'Bool','Bool','TruthValue','TruthValue']])
  (: direct-introduction-recursive-formula 
    (-> Bool Bool TruthValue TruthValue))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['direct-introduction-recursive-formula','False',_,['STV',PQs,PQc]],['STV',PQs,PQc])
  (= 
    (direct-introduction-recursive-formula False $_ 
      (STV $PQs $PQc)) 
    (STV $PQs $PQc))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['direct-introduction-recursive-formula','True','False',['STV',PQs,PQc]],['STV',['inc-count-strength',PQs,PQc],['inc-confidence',PQc]])
  (= 
    (direct-introduction-recursive-formula True False 
      (STV $PQs $PQc)) 
    (STV 
      (inc-count-strength $PQs $PQc) 
      (inc-confidence $PQc)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['direct-introduction-recursive-formula','True','True',['STV',PQs,PQc]],['STV',PQs,['inc-confidence',PQc]])
  (= 
    (direct-introduction-recursive-formula True True 
      (STV $PQs $PQc)) 
    (STV $PQs 
      (inc-confidence $PQc)))


; Evaluation took 1158.79 ms.
 Empty

  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[idi_axiom],['\x89\\x9E\',['\x86\\x92\',P,Q],['ETV','Empty',['PrCnt',1,0]]])
  (= 
    (idi_axiom) 
    ( 
      ( $P $Q) 
      (ETV Empty 
        (PrCnt 1 0))))


;; Recursive case (inductive rule):
;;
;; (p a)  patv
;; (q a)  qatv
;; pq  (ETV ev pqtv)
;; a  ev
;; 
;; pq  (ETV (insert a ev) tv)
;;
;; where tv is calculated as defined in the idi_formula.
;;
;; IDI rule as a function
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[idi_induction,['\x89\\x9E\',[P,A],Patv],['\x89\\x9E\',[Q,A],Qatv],['\x89\\x9E\',['\x86\\x92\',P,Q],['ETV',Ev,Pqtv]],['\x88\\x89\',A,Ev]],['\x89\\x9E\',['\x86\\x92\',P,Q],['ETV',[insert,A,Ev],[idi_formula,Patv,Qatv,Pqtv]]])
  (= 
    (idi_induction 
      ( 
        ($P $A) $Patv) 
      ( 
        ($Q $A) $Qatv) 
      ( 
        ( $P $Q) 
        (ETV $Ev $Pqtv)) 
      ( $A $Ev)) 
    ( 
      ( $P $Q) 
      (ETV 
        (insert $A $Ev) 
        (idi_formula $Patv $Qatv $Pqtv))))


; Corresponding matching query of IDI rule
;;; There is a bug with MeTTa interpreter in using let* for this matching query,
; as it matches ($p $a), ($q $a) with (= (idi_induction_match $kb) ...) pattern.
; Thus the interpreter gets in aninfinite loop. The solution given by Alexey is
; to set Type (:  (-> Atom Atom Atom)), but using such Type causes the evaluations
; inside the conclusion to don't get reduced. So, I am not using let* until gets fixed.
;;;
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,idi_induction_match,[->,Kb,'Atom']])
  (: idi_induction_match 
    (-> $Kb Atom))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[idi_induction_match,Kb],[match,Kb,[',',['\x89\\x9E\',[P,A],Patv],['\x89\\x9E\',[Q,A],Qatv],['\x89\\x9E\',['\x86\\x92\',P,Q],['ETV',Ev,Pqtv]],['\x88\\x89\',A,Ev]],[idi_induction,['\x89\\x9E\',[P,A],Patv],['\x89\\x9E\',[Q,A],Qatv],['\x89\\x9E\',['\x86\\x92\',P,Q],['ETV',Ev,Pqtv]],['\x88\\x89\',A,Ev]]])
  (= 
    (idi_induction_match $Kb) 
    (match $Kb 
      (and 
        ( 
          ($P $A) $Patv) 
        ( 
          ($Q $A) $Qatv) 
        ( 
          ( $P $Q) 
          (ETV $Ev $Pqtv)) 
        ( $A $Ev)) 
      (idi_induction 
        ( 
          ($P $A) $Patv) 
        ( 
          ($Q $A) $Qatv) 
        ( 
          ( $P $Q) 
          (ETV $Ev $Pqtv)) 
        ( $A $Ev))))


; Evaluation took 3.17 seconds.
 Empty

; Use IDI rule to infer P->Q based on the following,
;;; MeTTa port for deduction PLN rule
;;; using match
;;;
;;; ( P ptv)
;;; ( Q qtv)
;;; ( R rtv)
;;; ( ( P Q) tv1)
;;; ( ( Q R) tv2)
;;; 
;;; ( ( P R) TV)
;;;
;;; where ptv, qtv, rtv, tv1 and tv2 are truth values of the
;;; premises P, Q, R, ( P Q) and ( Q R) respectively.
;;; TV represents the resulting truth value of the conclusion.
;; Import formula functions
!(import! &self "../common/formula/DeductionFormula.metta")

%~ load_answer_file( '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/compat/match/DeductionImplicationDirectIntroductionMatchTest.metta.answers',
%~   '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/compat/match/DeductionImplicationDirectIntroductionMatchTest.metta')
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; Rule Definition ;;
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; Deduction rule represented as a function.
;;
;; P  PTV
;; Q  QTV
;; R  RTV
;; P  Q  PQTV
;; Q  R  RQTV
;; 
;; P  R  TV
;;; Formula and other functions used for the deduction rule
;; Import modules
!(import! &self "../truthvalue/TruthValue.metta")

      (min $U $X)))

;; Define approximately equal

  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'',[->,'Nat','Nat','Bool']])

  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'TruthValue','Type'])
  (: TruthValue Type)


;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; Constructors ;;
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; Boolean TV constructor
;; TODO: alternatively we could have (:  TruthValue) and (:  TruthValue)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'Bl',[->,'Bool','TruthValue']])
  (: Bl 
    (-> Bool TruthValue))


;; First order probability TV constructor, i.e. mere probability.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'Pr',[->,'Number','TruthValue']])
  (: Pr 
    (-> Number TruthValue))


;; Second order probability TV constructor, i.e. probability and
;; count.  The second order probability is distributed according to a
;; beta distribution.  The first argument of the constructor
;; represents the mode of the second order distribution.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'PrCnt',[->,'Number','Number','TruthValue']])
  (: PrCnt 
    (-> Number Number TruthValue))


;; Simple Truth Value.  A Second order probability TV constructor,
;; i.e. probability and confidence.  The probability is in fact the
;; mode of the corresponding beta distribution.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'STV',[->,'Number','Number','TruthValue']])
  (: STV 
    (-> Number Number TruthValue))


;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; Constants ;;
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; For now the underlying beta distributions have a Jeffreys prior,
;; i.e. the prior alpha and beta are 0.5.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,prior_alpha,[->,'Number']])
  (: prior_alpha 
    (-> Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[prior_alpha],0.5)
  (= 
    (prior_alpha) 0.5)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,prior_beta,[->,'Number']])
  (: prior_beta 
    (-> Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[prior_beta],0.5)
  (= 
    (prior_beta) 0.5)


;; Lookahead
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,lookahead,[->,'Number']])
  (: lookahead 
    (-> Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[lookahead],1.0)
  (= 
    (lookahead) 1.0)


;; Maximum supported count (till +inf is supported, possibly).
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'max-count',[->,'Number']])
  (: max-count 
    (-> Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['max-count'],1000000000.0)
  (= 
    (max-count) 1000000000.0)


;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; Methods ;;
;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; Convert count to confidence using the formula
;;
;; confidence = count / (count + lookahead)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'count->confidence',[->,'Number','Number']])
  (: count->confidence 
    (-> Number Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['count->confidence',Cnt],[/,Cnt,[+,Cnt,[lookahead]]])
  (= 
    (count->confidence $Cnt) 
    (/ $Cnt 
      (+ $Cnt 
        (lookahead))))


;; Convert confidence to count using the formula
;;
;; count = (confidence * lookahead) / (1 - confidence)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'confidence->count',[->,'Number','Number']])
  (: confidence->count 
    (-> Number Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['confidence->count',Conf],[if,[approxEq,1.0,Conf,1.0e-9],['max-count'],[/,[*,Conf,[lookahead]],[-,1.0,Conf]]])
  (= 
    (confidence->count $Conf) 
    (if 
      (approxEq 1.0 $Conf 1.0e-9) 
      (max-count) 
      (/ 
        (* $Conf 
          (lookahead)) 
        (- 1.0 $Conf))))


;; Increment the given count by 1
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'inc-count',[->,'Number','Number']])
  (: inc-count 
    (-> Number Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['inc-count',Cnt],[+,1,Cnt])
  (= 
    (inc-count $Cnt) 
    (+ 1 $Cnt))


;; Increment the corresponding count of the given confidence by 1 and
;; return the confidence of that corresponding incremented count.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'inc-confidence',[->,'Number','Number']])
  (: inc-confidence 
    (-> Number Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['inc-confidence',Conf],['count->confidence',['inc-count',['confidence->count',Conf]]])
  (= 
    (inc-confidence $Conf) 
    (count->confidence 
      (inc-count 
        (confidence->count $Conf))))


;; Return the strength of a truth value, given that its count has been
;; incremented by one but its positive count has not.
;;
;; The formula is derived from new_s = s*cnt / (cnt + 1), where cnt is
;; the count of the original truth value, that is cnt = c*k / (1-c).
;; Thus
;;
;; new_s = (s*c*k / (1-c)) / (c*k / (1-c) + 1)
;;       = (s*c*k / (1-c)) / ((c*k + 1-c) / (1-c))
;;       = (s*c*k) / (c*k + 1-c)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'inc-count-strength',[->,'Number','Number','Number']])
  (: inc-count-strength 
    (-> Number Number Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['inc-count-strength',S,C],[/,[*,S,[*,C,[lookahead]]],[-,[+,[*,C,[lookahead]],1],C]])
  (= 
    (inc-count-strength $S $C) 
    (/ 
      (* $S 
        (* $C 
          (lookahead))) 
      (- 
        (+ 
          (* $C 
            (lookahead)) 1) $C)))


;; Return the first order probability mode of the second order
;; distribution associated to a truth value.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,mode,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: mode 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mode,['Bl','True']],1.0)
  (= 
    (mode 
      (Bl True)) 1.0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mode,['Bl','False']],0.0)
  (= 
    (mode 
      (Bl False)) 0.0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mode,['Pr',Pr]],Pr)
  (= 
    (mode 
      (Pr $Pr)) $Pr)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mode,['PrCnt',Pr,_]],Pr)
  (= 
    (mode 
      (PrCnt $Pr $_)) $Pr)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mode,['STV',Pr,_]],Pr)
  (= 
    (mode 
      (STV $Pr $_)) $Pr)


;; Return the total count of a truth value.  For truth values not
;; capturing a notion of confidence, such as Bl or Pr then the count
;; is assumed to be a very large number (cause +inf does not seem to
;; be supported at the moment).  For truth values capturing a notion
;; of confidence, such as PrCnt, the total count is the count
;; component of the truth value.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,count,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: count 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[count,['Bl',_]],['max-count'])
  (= 
    (count 
      (Bl $_)) 
    (max-count))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[count,['Pr',_]],['max-count'])
  (= 
    (count 
      (Pr $_)) 
    (max-count))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[count,['PrCnt',_,Cnt]],Cnt)
  (= 
    (count 
      (PrCnt $_ $Cnt)) $Cnt)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[count,['STV',_,Conf]],['confidence->count',Conf])
  (= 
    (count 
      (STV $_ $Conf)) 
    (confidence->count $Conf))


;; Return the confidence of a truth value.  For truth values not
;; capturing a notion of confidence, such as Bl or Pr then the
;; confidence is assumed to be 1.0.  For truth values capturing a
;; notion of confidence, such as PrCnt, the formula to convert a count
;; into confidence is as follows
;;
;; confidence = count / (count + lookahead)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,confidence,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: confidence 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[confidence,['Bl',_]],1.0)
  (= 
    (confidence 
      (Bl $_)) 1.0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[confidence,['Pr',_]],1.0)
  (= 
    (confidence 
      (Pr $_)) 1.0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[confidence,['PrCnt',_,Cnt]],['count->confidence',Cnt])
  (= 
    (confidence 
      (PrCnt $_ $Cnt)) 
    (count->confidence $Cnt))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[confidence,['STV',_,Conf]],Conf)
  (= 
    (confidence 
      (STV $_ $Conf)) $Conf)


;; Return the positive count of a truth value.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,pos_count,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: pos_count 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[pos_count,Tv],[*,[mode,Tv],[count,Tv]])
  (= 
    (pos_count $Tv) 
    (* 
      (mode $Tv) 
      (count $Tv)))


;; Return the negative count of a truth value.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,neg_count,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: neg_count 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[neg_count,Tv],[*,[-,1,[mode,Tv]],[count,Tv]])
  (= 
    (neg_count $Tv) 
    (* 
      (- 1 
        (mode $Tv)) 
      (count $Tv)))


;; Return the posterior alpha of a truth value
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,post_alpha,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: post_alpha 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[post_alpha,Tv],[+,[prior_alpha],[pos_count,Tv]])
  (= 
    (post_alpha $Tv) 
    (+ 
      (prior_alpha) 
      (pos_count $Tv)))


;; Return the posterior beta of a truth value
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,post_beta,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: post_beta 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[post_beta,Tv],[+,[prior_beta],[neg_count,Tv]])
  (= 
    (post_beta $Tv) 
    (+ 
      (prior_beta) 
      (neg_count $Tv)))


;; Return the first order probability mean of the second order
;; distribution associated to a truth value.  For truth values not
;; capturing a notion of confidence, such as Bl or Pr then the
;; confidence is assumed to be 1.0.  For truth values capturing a
;; notion of confidence, such as PrCnt, a beta distribution is
;; assumed.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,mean,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])

;; Define max
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,max,[->,A,A,A]])

      (> $X $Y) $X $Y))

      (min $U $X)))
